## Idea

A type is `œÄ_n`-finite if it has finitely many connected components and all of its homotopy groups up to level `n` at all base points are finite.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="6781" class="Comment">-- Section 1. œÄ-Finiteness</a>

<a id="6809" class="Comment">-- Definition 1.3</a>

<a id="6828" class="Comment">-- We introduce locally finite types</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-Prop"></a><a id="6866" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6866" class="Function">is-locally-finite-Prop</a> <a id="6889" class="Symbol">:</a>
